Important News

141st Meeting of the Central Standing Committee

Recommended Liu Luxin and Others as Members of the Committee for Reviewing Writings Promoting Party Principles

Revised Outline of the Organizational Law for Provincial and County Representative Conferences

Those Expelled from the Party May Not Enjoy the Rights of Autonomous Citizens

The Central Headquarters of the Kuomintang held its 141st Standing Committee meeting on the 28th. Zhu Peide, Yu Youren, Ding Weifen, Ye Chucang, and Chiang Kai-shek attended. Wu Jingheng, Jiao Yitang, Zhou Qigang, Shao Yuanchong, Chen Guofu, Chen Lifu, Enke Batu, Fang Juehui, Yu Jingtang, Wang Boqun, Kexing'e, and Zeng Yangfu were present as observers. Zhu Peide chaired the meeting. The following resolutions were made: (1) Appointed Liu Zhennian, He Yisan, Han Dong, Li Wenjun, and An Yanzhi as the preparatory committee members of the special party department of the 21st Army. (2) Appointed Gong Bingfan, Wang Qinglong, Zhang Minquan, Wang Maode, Chai Qiaosong, Chen Houzai, and Zheng Qiufan as the preparatory committee members of the special party department of the 28th Army. (3) Appointed Zhang Changrong and Cao Jinming as additional preparatory committee members of the special party department of the 29th Army. (4) Recommended Liu Luxin, Ma Chaojun, Chen Bulei, Gui Chongji, and Cheng Tianfang as members of the Central Committee for Reviewing Writings Promoting Party Principles. (5) Stipulated that an agricultural association below the county or city level may be established in accordance with the law if more than half of its directly subordinate agricultural associations are formally established. A provincial agricultural association may be established in accordance with the law only when formally established agricultural associations exist in more than half of the counties and cities in the province. (6) Revised "The Organizational Law for Provincial and County Representative Conferences," Article 3, "The secretariat of the association designates a certain number of people" to "designate a certain number of working staff of the association." (7) Revised the decision of the 110th Standing Committee meeting regarding whether party members who have been expelled from the party or have had their party rights suspended can enjoy the rights of Article 7 of the Local Autonomy Implementation Law. The decision was that those expelled from the party may not enjoy the citizenship rights of Article 7 of the Township Autonomy Implementation Law and the right to be elected as the chiefs of townships, neighborhoods, and li. Those who have their party rights suspended cannot be compared with those expelled from the party. (8) Appointed Liu Mengxi as an additional member of the preparatory committee for the construction of the Cemetery for Fallen Martyrs. (9) Approved Comrade Xu Xinwu, director of the compilation section of the Central Organization Department, to resign, and appointed Comrade Hong Lanyou as the director of the compilation section of the Central Organization Department. (10) Appointed Comrade Wang Zixian as the secretary of the Central Relief Committee. (11) Recommended Committee Member Wu Jingheng to attend the Central Commemoration Week next Monday to report.

Gong and Guo Divisions

Bloody Battle to Attack the Bandit Lair in Donggu

Seizing Three Key Passes at the Gateway to Donggu

Red Bandits Counterattacked and Retreat Back to Ji'an

Gong Bingfan Has Returned to Nanchang to Report

Nanchang Correspondence: Since the Red bandit Peng Dehuai occupied Donggu, the residents within hundreds of miles around the constructed fortifications have been coerced to carry food into the mountains as a strategy of clearing the fields. Commander Gong Bingfan of the 28th Division was ordered to take charge of the main force attacking Donggu from Ji'an. Since the 17th, he led three regiments to attack Jiucun Ridge fiercely. He also sent a regiment to Guanyin Cliff to engage in fierce battles with Peng's bandits for two days and nights, killing many bandits. Later, Guo Huazong's division and Han's brigade joined the battle to assist. The bandit forces could not withstand it and retreated into the Donggu lair. Guanyin Cliff, Yantian Pit, and the key passes of Jiucun Ridge were occupied by Gong's division. Peng's bandits regarded these three key passes as the gateway to Donggu, so they launched a counterattack with all their might. The farmer bandits were in the front, and the gun bandits were in the back, advancing wave upon wave and fighting more and more fiercely. Gong's division was surrounded by bandits because it had penetrated deep into the bandit lair. They charged left and right, suffering considerable losses. Commander Gong was afraid of repeating the same mistakes of the 18th Division and retreated towards Futian. Unexpectedly, the bandits' momentum was fierce and they marched towards Ji'an. At the same time, the two Red bandit forces of Li Mingrui and Zeng Bingchun on the west bank of the Gan River also advanced from Yongxin towards the west of Ji'an, hoping to join forces with Peng's bandits to seize Ji'an. Fortunately, Tang's division in Jishui received the news and immediately sent Zhu's brigade to join the battle to provide support and consolidate the Ji'an defense line. At the same time, Hu Yixi's brigades of Luo's division marched from Taihe to the west of Ji'an, facing Li's bandits on one side and attacking Peng's bandits' waist on the other. The defense of Ji'an City was strictly guarded by Commander Luo and Zhang's brigade of Han's division. Therefore, no matter how many times the bandits charged, the government army's line did not change. The bandits began to be discouraged. Later, Han's division from Anfu and Hao's division from the fifth route reinforced Ji'an. Sun Lianzhong's troops also advanced from Le'an to Ji'an. The military strength was greatly enhanced, and the bandits retreated to Donggu. Yesterday, the 25th, Director He reported during the memorial week at the headquarters that although our army suffered more than 3,000 casualties in the Donggu battle, the number of Red bandits killed was more than 10,000. It is conceivable how fierce the battle was. According to news from the Ji'an postal sector, when Gong's division retreated to Ji'an, the Red bandits once advanced to an area 30 li away from Ji'an City. After Han's division and Hao's division arrived, the situation turned from danger to safety. Commander Gong has retreated to the rear for rest due to heavy losses. Deputy Commander Wang Xiangding of the Sixth Route Army and Commander Gong arrived in the province from Ji'an yesterday to report the battle to Director He. Director He expressed his condolences to Wang and Gong and promised to provide sufficient reinforcements. However, according to Commander Gong's report, the defeat was actually caused by his chief of staff Zhang Minquan's wrong measures and improper deployment. Therefore, Zhang was arrested and handed over to the Public Security Bureau for punishment. In recent days, the Red bandits have been in a stalemate with the government army in the southeast area of Ji'an. Han's and Hao's divisions have replaced Gong's and Guo's divisions in defending the line of Ji'an, Taihe, and Yongfeng. There have been no major battles. However, four aircraft of the 5th Aviation Squadron have been flying to the vicinity of Donggu for bombing operations. According to aviation personnel reports, more than ten bombs were dropped in Donggu today, all hitting and exploding, killing many bandits. (27th)

Hubei Provincial Government Reorganized in Compliance with Orders

New Provincial Committee Scheduled to Take Office on June 1st

Hankou Correspondence: The news about the reorganization of the Hubei Provincial Government has been circulating for a long time but has not been realized. It was not until the State Council held a state affairs meeting on the 26th of this month that a decision was made. He Chengjun will continue to serve as chairman, Liu Wendao will serve as director of the Department of Civil Affairs, Wu Guozhen will serve as director of the Department of Finance, Fang Dazhi will continue to concurrently serve as director of the Department of Construction, and Huang Jianzhong will continue to concurrently serve as director of the Department of Education. Zhu Huaibing, Ma Dengying, Peng Jieshi, and Chen Guangzu will serve as committee members. The central government will still appoint former Director of Civil Affairs Wu Xingya as the director of the Department of Civil Affairs of Anhui, former Committee Member Xiong Bingkun will be transferred to serve as a military counselor to the National Government, and Xie Lü will be transferred to serve as a counselor to the Military Council. Wu and others are scheduled to leave Hankou for Beijing within a few days. The members of the provincial party department, representatives from all walks of life, and all staff members of the Department of Civil Affairs are scheduled to hold a farewell meeting for Wu Xingya at the Puhai Chun on the 28th to leave a memento. Except for Chairman He Chengjun, who is staying in Beijing, and Committee Member Ma Dengying, who is in Shashi defending the second front, and Committee Member Zhu Huaibing, who is in Macheng defending the second front, the rest of the new committee members are in Hankou. It is rumored that a swearing-in ceremony will be held on June 1st. The Departments of Civil Affairs and Finance have been rushing to complete the handover in recent days and are very busy. It is expected that the handover will be completed by the end of this month. The reporter interviewed the new Director of Civil Affairs Liu Wendao and the new Director of Finance Wu Guozhen yesterday and had a brief conversation with them. Liu said that he had only seen in the newspaper that he had been appointed as a member of the provincial committee and director of the Department of Civil Affairs, and had not yet received a clear order. He will wait for the central government to issue a clear order and for Chairman He to return to Hubei before he can schedule his inauguration. He cannot talk about the policy direction at the moment. He plans to first investigate the actual situation before determining a plan to proceed. As for the municipal government, it cannot be taken care of at the same time. The central government should have a solution to this, so he is still maintaining the status quo. Wu said that Hubei's finances have reached the point of extreme difficulty. Chairman He is currently discussing this matter with the central government in Beijing. He will discuss the plan with him after Chairman He returns to Hankou, and consider the situation to determine a solution to ensure that revenue and expenditure are balanced. The deficit of more than 2 million yuan in the provincial treasury will also be gradually repaid. (May 27th)

Hankou Headquarters Circular

Strictly Prevent Red Bandits from Purchasing Weapons in Hankou

Two Criminals Selling Bullets Executed by Firing Squad

Hankou Correspondence: The Wuhan Headquarters previously reported that the source of firearms and ammunition for the Red bandits in Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi was mostly purchased from the Hankou Concession, and ordered the Detective Office to strictly investigate and arrest them. Recently, the office discovered that a German merchant's foreign company was privately selling 15,000 rounds of ammunition to the Red bandits. It was seized and confiscated, and a protest was lodged with the German Consulate. At the same time, Li Yunheng, commander of the 53rd Division, reported that most of the firearms and ammunition of the Red bandits in Henan Province were also purchased from Hankou, and requested that measures be taken to strictly prevent them from being smuggled out of the country. The Headquarters considered the matter to be of great importance and issued a circular to all troops on the 27th to prevent it, and executed Wang Qingjie, Hu Kaisheng, and other criminals who sold ammunition to support the Red bandits by firing squad on the same day to warn the public. The charges are recorded as follows: (1) Public Notice: According to the Detective Office's transfer of Wang Qingjie, a criminal who sold ammunition to support the Red bandits, for interrogation, the Military Law Department of this Headquarters has determined that the criminal Wang Qingjie directly sold ammunition three times and provided security for Zhang Tuhua of the false provincial committee and Yang Guanghua, who handled the ammunition. The self-confessed persons have identified them one by one, and the criminal has also directly admitted it. Such a willing affiliation with bandits is an unforgivable crime, and it should be punished with the death penalty in accordance with Article 5, paragraph 1 of the Emergency Law for Punishing Endangering the Republic of China to warn others. In addition to ordering that the criminal Wang Qingjie be bound and sent to the execution ground to be executed by firing squad, this public notice is hereby issued to inform the public. (2) Public Notice: According to the Detective Office's transfer of Hu Kaisheng and others, criminals who purchased ammunition for the bandits, for interrogation, the Military Law Department of this Headquarters has determined that the criminal Hu Kaisheng confessed that he colluded with Wang Tianhong, a procurer stationed in Hankou for the bandit army in Hanchuan, and entrusted Jiang Haishan to purchase ammunition in succession in the name of the Hanchuan team, and delivered it to the traffic office of the bandit army in Huajing Street. The self-confessed persons have certified it in court, proving that such willing affiliation with bandits is indeed an unforgivable crime and should be punished with the death penalty in accordance with Article 5, paragraph 1 of the Emergency Law for Punishing Endangering the Republic of China to warn others. In addition to ordering that the criminal Hu Kaisheng be bound and sent to the execution ground to be executed by firing squad, this public notice is hereby issued to inform all people. (May 27th)

Suxian County Magistrate Forcibly Levies Opium Tax

Poisonous Flowers Occupy Two-Thirds of the County's Land

County Magistrate Forces Each District to Pay 300,000 Yuan in Tax

Bengbu Correspondence: The counties of Su, Meng, Wo, and Hao in northern Anhui have long been known as the most prominent areas for opium production, exporting no less than several million taels annually, poisoning various provinces and causing endless harm. Among them, Suxian County plants the most. Recently, poppies have flourished and filled the fields. It is estimated that the county has more than 180 villages, and each village plants tens of hectares of opium seedlings. Therefore, poisonous flowers occupy nearly two-thirds of the county's land. This alarming number has aroused the covetousness of the county authorities. Although various districts want to implement eradication, the county government forcibly retains the opium seedlings to apportion the seedling tax. First, they ordered each district to register the acreage and report it to the county government. County Magistrate Wang Xinlan recently convened a meeting of the ten district chiefs in the county government and ordered them to acknowledge and pay 300,000 yuan in opium seedling tax. The district chiefs argued that the county had suffered repeated banditry, war disasters, and the people were impoverished, making it difficult to bear the burden. Because they did not agree, Wang sent teams to monitor them and force them to sign. Yesterday evening (the 26th), the district chiefs took the opportunity to escape from the county government and took the Jinpu express train to Bengbu. This morning (the 27th), they presented a petition to the Northern Anhui Garrison Headquarters, requesting a halt to the tax levy. The Chief of Staff received them and promised to send a telegram to stop it immediately. At 12 o'clock, the district chiefs were hosted by the district party headquarters to meet with the press. Lu Qixun, the district chief of the ninth district, reported the details of the incident, stating that since County Magistrate Wang Xinlan took office last winter, various measures have been out of sync with public opinion. The most prominent is protecting corrupt gentry, shielding communist party members, selling and releasing bandits, banning the eradication of opium seedlings, and harming the people in violation of the law, which is rare among administrative officials. He also said that opium seedlings are the people's lifeblood, and no district is allowed to eradicate them; violators will be shot. Recently, each district chief was forced to acknowledge 300,000 yuan in opium seedling tax, with a deadline for payment. Those who did not agree would be placed under surveillance. Because they were unwilling to sign, they were placed under house arrest and risked escaping yesterday. Wang sent bailiffs to search and arrest them, chasing them to the train station, but they had already boarded the train and were not caught. Fortunately, he also said that in addition to sending telegrams to the central government and the provincial government to state their case, they also planned to go to Beijing tonight to appeal to the central government, and then go to Anqing to request the provincial government to quickly send a telegram to stop the extortion and request Wang's removal and punishment to appease public anger. The telegrams from the district chiefs and district preparatory staff to the central government and the Anhui government are recorded as follows: "To the Nanjing Central Party Headquarters, the National Government, the Control Yuan, the Executive Yuan, the Opium Prohibition Committee, the Anhui Provincial Government, and the Provincial Party Headquarters: Wang Xinlan, the County Magistrate of Suxian County, Anhui Province, has violated the national ban by forcibly retaining opium seedlings, levying a registration fee of 30,000 yuan, and forcing district chiefs and others to acknowledge an opium seedling tax of 300,000 yuan, to be paid by June 15. The county has deducted 10,000 yuan from the public funds paid by each district as a registration fee. The district chiefs and others were forced to secretly leave Suxian and go to Beijing and the province to petition. We hereby telegraph this matter urgently, begging your excellency to quickly send a telegram to stop this in order to maintain the national ban. We await your orders urgently. Respectfully, Li Xinming, District Chief of the First District of Suxian County; Chen Zhujiu, Preparatory Staff of the Second District; Chang Faming, District Chief of the Third District; Zhang Jianxun, District Chief of the Fourth District; Chen Yulun, Preparatory Staff of the Fifth District; Zhou Bingzhi, Preparatory Staff of the Sixth District; Zhong Jincun, Preparatory Staff of the Eighth District; Lu Qixun, District Chief of the Ninth District; Sun Xiaozu, District Chief of the Tenth District. Respectfully kowtow. (27th)"

Recent Situation of the Jinbei Mining Bureau

Currently Has More Than 1,000 Workers

Daily Coal Output Exceeds 300 Tons

Taiyuan Correspondence: The Jinbei Mining Bureau was established in May of the 18th year of the Republic (1929) as a joint public-private enterprise with a fully paid-up capital of 1 million yuan. The general bureau is located in Datong County. The general manager, Dang Gechun, is from Jin County, Shanxi Province, and graduated from Shanxi University and the Mining Department of Waseda University in Japan. The general bureau organization consists of five departments: general affairs, engineering, accounting, business, and road affairs. There are also offices and hospitals in various locations, as well as a mine police management office. The road affairs department has an office in Kouquan, and the engineering department has offices under the two mines, further divided into six sections: well affairs, machinery, materials, surveying and mapping, accounting, and miscellaneous affairs, totaling more than 100 employees. Currently, there are two mining areas: Yongdingzhuang and Meiyukou. The highest authority of the mining bureau is the fundraising committee, which is responsible for supervision and management. The Datong Qingyan coal is hard, dense, has high calorific value, and very little ash and sulfur content. Although it has a small amount of Qingyan, the black smoke does not stick at all, making it ideal for factories and ships. Each mine has two vertical shafts, and coal is extracted in three shifts per day. Each shift has an average of about 400 workers. Currently, due to the shortage of train cars on the PingSui Railway, transportation is extremely difficult, so exports are temporarily restricted, with only 300 tons being produced per day. It is expected that when everything returns to normal and the mines are roughly in place, a daily output of 2,000 tons will not be difficult. The Yongdingzhuang mining area covers more than 89 acres, with two minable coal seams. The first layer is about 180 feet from the surface and about five feet thick. The second layer is about 350 feet from the surface and about eight feet thick. Currently, the first coal seam is being mined. The Meiyukou mine currently has a mining area of about 10 square miles, with two minable coal seams. One is about 300 feet deep and eight feet thick, and the other is about 700 feet deep and ten feet thick. Currently, the first coal seam is also being mined. Underground coal mining uses a contract system. The contract price for digging one foot of the main tunnel is currently 3.1 yuan, and the contract price for digging one foot of the coal cave is currently 2.6 yuan. The main tunnel is about one zhang wide, and the coal cave is about eight chi wide. There are nine types of workers in total, namely: coolies, factory workers, outside factory workers, machinists, carpenters (monthly wages), carpenters (daily wages), road workers, machinery repair factory machinists, road affairs department machinists, and escort coolies. The total number of workers is about 1,000. The highest wage is 48 yuan, and the lowest is 8 yuan. Regarding transportation, Kouquan is 36 li away from Datong. After the PingSui branch line was built in the 7th year of the Republic (1918), it began to transport coal. In addition, there is the Meiquan Railway, which runs from Kouzhen to Meiyukou, and the Yongquan Railway, which runs from Kouquan Town to Yongdingzhuang. Both roads are connected to the Tongquan branch line, making transportation quite convenient. These two roads were built by the Jinbei Mining Bureau itself. The Quanquan Railway is also directly under the jurisdiction of the Jinbei Mining Bureau. It is a small railway with a gauge about one-third smaller than ordinary railway tracks. The carriages and locomotives are also very narrow, and each time it can only transport a maximum of 40 tons of coal, specifically for transporting coal to the surrounding soil kilns. Sales locations include Pingjin, Gu, Hu, Han, Qingdao, Japan, etc. The value per ton varies due to freight and other factors. (May 23)

Guangzhou

Unresolved Case of the Tram Company Resolved

Municipal Government Passes Five Measures to Terminate the Contract

Establish a Liquidation Committee to Recompense Shareholders' Capital

In the 13th year of the Republic (1924), the Yue Tram Company signed a contract with the government to lay tracks and operate trams in the urban area. At that time, the tram company reported a contribution of 1 million Hong Kong dollars to the government's military expenses. The government then specially granted the company various rights. Subsequently, after repeated political changes, the company also suspended operations due to financial constraints. The Guangzhou Municipal Government recently decided that if the company continued in this way, it would not only hinder the development of road administration, but also greatly damage the company's capital. Therefore, it was decided to send personnel to take over the company and carry out reorganization. Recently, the company's contract was cancelled. The measures for terminating the contract have been approved by the 36th Municipal Administrative Conference. The measures for terminating the tram company's contract are recorded as follows: (1) The 20-year approval period for the company is counted from eight months after September 20, the 13th year of the Republic (1924), which is the date of the order. According to the scheduled deadline, May 20, the 14th year of the Republic (1925), is the deadline. By May 20 of this year, six years have passed. The 1 million Hong Kong dollars that were reported as a contribution to the government should be amortized evenly over 20 years, accounting for 50,000 yuan per year, totaling 300,000 yuan for six years. After the contract is terminated, in addition to deducting the amount, 700,000 yuan should be returned. (2) The case of the company paying interest on the 1 million yuan to the government in installments was jointly reviewed and reported by the Public Works and Utilities Bureaus on November 23 of a certain year of the Republic, stating that the company had not built tram roads for a long time and did not comply with the contract. The government should not deliver the interest on the contribution already paid. This point should not be discussed. (3) The amount to be returned after deducting the contribution after the contract is terminated is quite large. A section of land with a corresponding value in the Haizhu Inner Port should be designated and ordered to be reserved by the Finance Bureau for future investment and compensation. (4) The company's general manager, Wu Yuhan, and supervisor, Wu Jiepan, have already issued resignation reports to the shareholders. In order to protect the rights of the company's shareholders, a liquidation committee should be established immediately to carry out all liquidation work and notify all shareholders to register within a time limit so that funds can be distributed proportionally in the future. (5) The original contract was signed and sealed by the former military governor, the provincial governor, and the former municipal office director. The procedures for terminating the contract should first be submitted to the provincial government for approval before being processed in order to comply with the procedures. (May 23)

Shenyang City Holds Large-Scale Health Campaign

Shenyang Correspondence: The Shenyang Municipal Office, in conjunction with various agencies and organizations, held a health campaign conference and established a preparatory committee. Seven meetings were held and it was decided to hold a grand health campaign and parade lectures on the 16th, 17th, and 18th of this month to arouse public awareness. The details of the conference are described below:

Exhibition: Prior to the conference, the association constructed a pine branch archway in front of the Qingnianhui Qian Hutung west entrance inside the Dananmen, decorated with five-colored electric lights and a white cloth with the nine characters "Shenyang City Health Campaign Conference" suspended in the middle, and prepared triangular small paper flags to be distributed to citizens by the city's labor unions and chambers of commerce to hang. Cloth plaques were hung and slogans printed by the Municipal Office at each city gate and traffic thoroughfare. Each report released a special health supplement. The east and west halls of the Youth Association were requisitioned by the Nanman Medical University and Chinese classmates to collect various specimens, instruments, models, and other items related to health and medicine and displayed separately from 9:00 AM to 3:00 PM each day to allow people to enter and view them. Professors from the Liaoning Medical College and other schools were on hand to provide guidance at any time. It is estimated that nearly 20,000 to 30,000 men and women from the city visited during the three days.

Lectures: The association was scheduled to hold lectures in the Youth Association gym from 6:00 PM to 9:00 PM every evening. After the lectures, health films, new dramas, magic shows, and other entertainment were screened. Admission tickets were available for anyone to obtain. The speakers on the first day were Gao Moquan and Liu Zhongming from the Liaoning Medical College. On the second day, they were Li Quancheng and Guo Guangwu from the Manchuria Medical University. On the third day, they were Wang Yougang and Dong Bingran from the Tongshan Medical College. Each lecture was designed to promote practical application of their theory, and so, after 5:00 PM each day, people came to listen.

Parade: The association was scheduled to hold a parade on the second day. Prior to the parade, a temporary mat shed was built directly north of the Xiaoheyan Public Sports Field, with a cloth sign reading "Shenyang City Health Campaign Conference" hanging at the entrance, as a gathering point for various agencies, organizations, and citizens to participate in the parade. On the morning of the 17th, Liu Guozeng, the head of the sanitation department of the Municipal Office, led his colleagues to the venue to take care of matters. Before long, personnel from various agencies and organizations below the provincial government, merchants, citizens, students from various schools, Boy Scouts, and public security teams.

Page 8

Decorated publicity vehicles arrived one after another. Each agency and organization had a large flag, and each person held a small flag with health slogans written on it. At 10:00 AM, when all the participants had arrived, Chen Bolin and Zhang Songjun climbed onto a high table and used a megaphone to organize the ranks. After the ranks were organized, Xiong Fei, the commander-in-chief, gave the order, and the parade started amidst the music of the Bian Shu Orchestra. The mighty parade route started from Xiaoheyan, entered Dadongmen, passed through Siping Street Gulou, exited Daximen, and went all the way to the South Market. Along the way, the public security bureau's decorated publicity vehicles were decorated with models of rice buckets, dung buckets, flies, etc., and a paper-mache pig, vividly portraying the pig's mouth spitting out promotional materials at any time to attract the attention of the audience. The Changshi Promotion Association's decorated publicity vehicle was led by the association's president, Che Xiangchen, who led members in performing lung disease and various infectious diseases from unsanitary food and fly transmission to warn the citizens. It is estimated that more than 10,000 people participated, and the streets were packed with people. The parade did not disperse until 3:00 PM. Slogans: "Pay attention to personal hygiene," "Pay attention to public hygiene," "Hygiene promotes health," "Unsanitary conditions are suicide," "Hygiene and disease prevention," "Hygiene prolongs life," "Eliminate flies," "Defeat tuberculosis," "Eliminate dirt," "Clean homes."

Local Correspondence

Kunshan

Another Kidnapping Case at Xiema Bridge: Wu Yunzhou, a resident of Xiema Bridge and Shangbang in the county, was wealthy and coveted by kidnappers. He was previously targeted for kidnapping last year, but fortunately, Wu was not at home at the time, and the bandits kidnapped his uncle, Yin Zhai, who escaped safely afterward. Two bandit ships arrived at the location again the other day, with more than 20 bandits on board. After landing, they each held guns and swarmed into Wu's residence, kidnapping Wu Yunzhou and relatives Zhang Puren and a Chen-surname man and woman, and taking them to a boat on the Dianshan Lake. Afterwards, the Wu family did not report to the county government, nor did they receive any news from the bandits.

Wuxi

Silk Cocoon Association's Membership Fee Issue: The regular expenses of the local silk cocoon industry association were previously collected by the silk cocoon tax bureau at a rate of three cents per dan of dried cocoons, with two cents retained for the association's regular expenses and one cent transferred to the Shanghai Su Zhe Wan Silk Cocoon General Association to fund expenses. After the political opening in the 16th year of the Republic (1927), the one cent for the General Association was directly claimed from the Department of Finance, without being transferred through Wuxi. This year, the silk cocoon tax bureau was abolished, making it impossible to collect the tax. The Silk Cocoon Association raised the issue during a meeting the other day and initially planned to collect three cents per dan of fresh cocoons, following the Liyang method. After discussion, it was decided to collect a membership fee of five cents per dan of fresh cocoons, with three dan of fresh cocoons being equivalent to one dan of dried cocoons, totaling an actual collection of fifteen cents. The one cent for the Shanghai General Association will be discussed later. The business tax for cocoon stoves will continue to be collected at one yuan as before, and the newly established business tax will be petitioned for exemption.

Building a Boat Shed Leads to a Riot: The Minfeng Silk Factory in Yaozhuangbang, outside the South Gate of the city, planned to build a gasoline boat shed on the riverbank, which was obstructed by villagers such as Zhu Xiaodi. Zhou Jiashan, the head of the eighth sub-bureau of the public security bureau in charge of the area, fearing that incidents would occur, sent bureau member Cao and four policemen to suppress the situation. However, when they arrived at the factory, more than 300 villagers had already gathered. Cao tried to persuade the crowd, but the villagers had poor knowledge and a misunderstanding occurred, leading to a severe beating of Cao, causing serious injuries. Four rifles were also seized. Later, the third sub-bureau of the public security bureau and the police brigade headquarters were telegraphed to request police assistance. Wang, the head of the Wang sub-bureau, and Wang, the captain of the brigade, immediately dispatched armed police teams upon receiving the report. However, the villagers remained defiant. Seeing this, the police team fired several shots into the sky as a warning and carried out arrests, immediately detaining Zhu Xiaodi and Chen Fengquan, the two ringleaders. The seized firearms were also recovered and sent to the public security bureau. Yesterday, they were transferred to the county court for legal proceedings.

Negotiating to Increase Business Tax Assessment: The county chamber of commerce previously convened a meeting of various industries to discuss and determine the method of paying the business tax. Each industry reported its business volume and the number of payments separately, which were verified and reviewed by industry leaders appointed by the chamber of commerce. It is estimated that more than 40,000 gold were identified. The other day, Yang Wubian, the director of the business tax bureau, was ordered by the Department of Finance to invite Qian Sunqing, the chairman of the chamber of commerce, to go to the Department of Finance to discuss the matter properly. Qian was unable to go due to other matters, and Yang returned to Wuxi yesterday. The Department of Finance believes that the assessed amount for each industry is too disparate and needs to be persuaded to increase it again. However, each industry believes that the silk industry is hopeless and the market is even more sluggish, making it impossible to increase the amount in fact. Director Yang has already informed the county chamber of commerce to notify various industries to gather at the chamber of commerce at 2:00 PM today (the 29th) for a discussion to negotiate a reasonable increase in the assessed amount to respect the wishes of the provincial government.

Jiangyin

The Local Court Investigates Li Leng's Bribery Case: Cai Dingcheng, a prosecutor of the Wu County Local Court, was ordered by the High Court to investigate the bribery and opium case of Li Leng, the former magistrate of Jiangyin, and has scheduled a hearing. Because the files of the cases of Mafeiqian Zhulang in Yueqiao Township, broken by the Public Security Bureau, and the cases of Qian Abao and others broken by Yang Bingwei, the opium investigation team leader, need to be reviewed, he sent a letter to the Public Security Bureau yesterday requesting them to send them for reference.

The Relief Institute Illegally Refuses News Interviews: Cao Yuanpu, the director of the Relief Institute, is collecting fish donation taxes for charity. He is now under instructions from the Provincial Government to implement the Ministry of Industry's instructions to actively promote the fishing industry, and all fish taxes and fish industry taxes are exempt. In the future, no agency shall establish other names to collect these donations. Because the Relief Institute did not comply with the order after receiving it, it had to wait until the current season's first quarter was collected before it could be published. On the 25th, the Jiangsheng Dasheng News reported that the fish industry had informed the fishmongers to stop collecting the taxes. Director Cao was angry with the two newspapers. Yesterday (the 26th), he ordered the staff to refuse interviews with the two newspaper reporters and stop their advertisements. The two newspaper editors believe that the Relief Institute is a local charitable organization and that this kind of illegal prejudice is suppressing public opinion. They are currently devising methods to deal with it in order to show justice.

Zhenjiang

Submitting a Petition to Severely Punish the Notorious Bandit Chen Wenqi: The Zhenjiang County Executive Committee held its 68th executive committee meeting yesterday to discuss the notorious bandit Chen Wenqi, who repeatedly burned, killed, and kidnapped in the four villages. He was previously captured by the county government and fled. He has now been escorted to the province in Hangzhou. Should we request that he be severely punished according to the law to eliminate bandits? It was decided to submit a petition to the province and forward it to the provincial government for legal action to serve as a warning.

Japanese Ships Continue to Intrude on Fishing Grounds: In order to protect the coastal fishing industry in Jiangsu Province, the Provincial Government previously convened a fisheries protection conference. Regarding the prevention of foreign ships intruding on fishing grounds, two measures were discussed and decided, including the fact that the Agriculture and Mining Department should report the intrusion of Japanese fishing boats at any time based on the information obtained, and the Provincial Government ordered the Agriculture Department to comply. According to the department's investigation, since May 1 of this year, there are still 12 ships, including Man Qian Wan and Zhou Fang Wan, entering and leaving Shanghai and Hong Kong to sell their catches. In addition, there are more than 20 ships, including Da Cheng Wan, which previously intruded on fishing grounds. Fearing that the Chinese customs will prohibit imports on schedule, they are temporarily waiting to see. If this situation is not resolved in the shortest possible time, the influx of Japanese ships into Shanghai will be inevitable. It is reported that the department has submitted reports to the Provincial Government and the Ministry of Industry for verification.

Yangzhou

News of School Strikes: The schools in Jiangdu County have been on strike for more than three days due to funding issues. However, the content of this strike is not entirely consistent. Some have completely stopped, some have only stopped elementary classes and not high school classes, some are uniformly studying at school, and some are attending classes as usual. Therefore, some teachers and staff who advocate a thorough strike went to the schools that have not stopped classes today (the 27th) to persuade them to take unified action. However, it is heard that some teachers and staff believe that the sixth-grade students will be graduating soon, and it is impossible to stop classes completely. As for the salary issue, everyone unanimously agrees. However, the administrative side is planning in every possible way, and by the latest deadline of the abolished Dragon Boat Festival, they can only issue one and a half months' worth of salaries. There is no other way. The teachers and staff held another meeting today (the 27th) to discuss whether to resume classes immediately. There is no definite news yet.

Opium Suspect Resists Arrest and Assaults Police Officers: Gao Jichun, the head of the seventh sub-bureau of the public security bureau, received a report from Chen Bingyan, a resident of Chenjiadian, that Chen Yuanxing and Chen Yuanyi were selling large quantities of opium and that Wang Dajie was running an opium den. He sent inspector Liao Dingjie to lead the police with the original reporter to investigate. When they arrived at Chen Yuanxing's house, they found evidence of opium, lamps, and guns. The Chen family closed the door and rang the gong to gather a crowd to seize the evidence, tear the police uniforms, and beat the inspector and secret agent Wang Yaozhang on the head, causing them to bleed profusely. The reporter was also injured and had his pistol and watch stolen. Yesterday (the 26th), he reported the situation to the public security bureau for investigation.

Gaoyou

Four Bandits Captured in the Sixth District: Gao Jinkui, the leader of the 25th team of the 6th district of the water public security team stationed in Jieshouzhen, inspected a steamer in the town the other day and captured four bandits on the Qingzhen Changban small steamer. They were escorted to the city last night and sent to the 6th district for interrogation.

A Kidnapping Case Occurs in Nan'an Township: Five bandits suddenly arrived at the home of Chen Lianggui, the head of Nan'an Township in the fifth district of the county, at about 8:00 PM the other day. They each held guns and lured open the door to enter and loot extensively. Before leaving, they also kidnapped his daughter-in-law, Ms. Wang. He immediately reported to the Laorenqiao Police Team, which was stationed there. Squad leader Wang led a team to arrest the bandits, but they had already escaped without a trace. Township Head Chen has come to the city to petition the county government to strictly investigate.

Nantong

Relocating the Wounded Soldiers' Factory Resolved by the Headquarters: All sectors of Tong County oppose the conversion of the poor people's factory into the Eleventh Fake Wounded Soldiers' Factory. The county government has telegraphed the provincial government to appeal for relocation to another location. On the 27th, County Magistrate Zhang received a reply from the provincial government stating that the telegram had been forwarded to the headquarters. It has been approved by Luo, the division commander of the 24th Division of the Army, in a telegram on the 25th, stating that Zhao Jianhua, the director of the relief institute, instigated the crowd to insult soldiers and seized weapons from the guards. The squad leader was also robbed when he went out to buy food. He requested strict punishment. If this is the case, it should be dealt with promptly and conveyed to all organizations to wait for instructions and not cause trouble. Because all sectors are extremely angry about the wounded soldiers' factory, County Magistrate Zhang specifically went to the province on the 28th to personally present everything to Chairman Ye.

Military Police Inspect Japanese Ships and Negotiate: The Nissin Shipping Company stated that in recent months, the Xiangyang, Fengyang, and Luoyang ships were ordered to stop for inspection when they passed through the Nantong Lujing Port by military police firing guns from small steamers, causing negotiations. On the 27th, the Department of Civil Affairs ordered the Nantong County Government to investigate the matter thoroughly and submit a fair report for verification.

Ningbo

Verdict in the Case of a Prostitute Dying from Abortion: Xiao Lin Suzhen, a prostitute at the Eryi Xiaozhu brothel in Houshi, Yong, had beautiful looks and was only 14 years old. General customers of pleasure all flocked to her. The prostitute secretly conspired with the customer and became pregnant. Fearing that her pregnant belly would affect her business, the prostitute’s room attendant, Zhu Fengbao, and the pimp, Zhu Fusheng, advocated calling the midwife, Xie Li, to use medicine to induce an abortion. Her biological mother, Lin Le, also did not stop her. Unexpectedly, the bleeding did not stop after the abortion, and she died three days later. The Yinxian Local Court Prosecutor’s Office heard about it and filed a report, ordering a group of witnesses to appear in court for investigation. Zhu Fengbao and Zhu Fusheng fled upon hearing the news, and Xie Li and Lin Le were sent to prison separately. The prosecutor then filed a public prosecution. Yesterday, the criminal court of the court ruled that the defendant, Xie Li, was guilty of deliberately profiting and causing an abortion that resulted in death and was sentenced to three years of imprisonment. The defendant, Lin Le, was guilty of requesting an abortion that resulted in death and was sentenced to three years of imprisonment. The trial proceedings for Zhu Fengbao and Zhu Fusheng were suspended.

Killing a Bandit Leader and Capturing Three Bandits: Sun Zhengfu of Shijiaoqiu, Xixiang, Yuyao, was kidnapped by bandits on the 25th of this month and extorted 500 yuan. He pleaded and was eventually extorted 200 yuan. Since it was late at night and there was nowhere to raise the money, he first paid 78 yuan and limited the remaining amount to be paid at the Caijia Road Barracks Head at 5:00 PM the next afternoon. The third battalion of the Yuyao Security Team was informed of this and sent detectives Zhang Xinmei, together with Xie Alang, the squad leader of the Niqiaolu Defense Corps, and more than ten others, to go to the payment location with Sun Zhengfu. They saw eight bandits coming. The two sides exchanged fire. Farmers from nearby villages also heard the sound and came out to assist in the pursuit. The bandit leader Niu Zhangbao was killed and bandits Wang Jinsheng, Xu Aliang, and Wang Ahai were captured. Corpsman Li Jifa and two farmers were also shot and wounded. The three captured bandits have now been escorted to the cleansing bureau for review.

Xinghua

The Death of Classical Prose Scholar Li Shengyan: Li Shengyan, a scholar of our county, was famous for his classical prose. His students were all over the world. He once served as a lecturer at the Central University and a writer at the Central Research Institute. Many high-ranking officials and old friends. He never dabbled in an official career in his life. In recent years, he lived in seclusion in Linquan and wrote behind closed doors. Unexpectedly, he died of stomach disease at 3:00 PM on May 17th. He was 73 years old. People from far away sent their condolences in succession. People at the time lamented that another weakness had taken root in the domestic literary world.

North China Sports Federation Annual Meeting

Jinan, 28th - The North China Annual Meeting was held at 7:00 PM on the 28th at Qing Hui. The amended charter is as follows: Article 1: The name of this association is the North China Sports Federation. Article 2: The purpose of this association is to promote sports in North China and to promote the national spirit. Article 3: The area under the jurisdiction of this association shall be the following provinces, cities, and districts: 1. Provinces: Hebei, Henan, Shandong, Shanxi, Shaanxi, Gansu, Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, Rehe, Chahar, Suiyuan, Xinjiang, Ningxia; 2. Cities: Beiping, Qingdao; 3. Special District of Dong Province. Article 4: The association shall (1) organize various competitive sports events; (2) assist and promote the organization and development of local sports federations within the association's area; (3) organize various research associations related to sports. The following matters were not discussed and will be continued tomorrow. It is scheduled to open at 7:00 AM on the 31st at the North China Reception Office. Please have each province and city's chief coach, instructor, and athlete review the troops. Furthermore, the North China Meeting will be held once every two years thereafter.

Liu Changchun's Performance Dims

Mediocre Results in 100 Meters and 400 Meters

Forfeits 200 Meters Due to Leg Injury

Jinan, 28th - Liu Changchun forfeits this afternoon's men's senior 200-meter final.

Jinan, 28th - Liu Changchun wins the men's senior 100 meters and 400 meters, but his 100-meter time is 11.8 seconds and his 400-meter time is 54.3/10 seconds, a significant decline from his previous performances. Meanwhile, the men's intermediate 100-meter time is 11.7 seconds. Although Liu Changchun has fallen to second place in sprinting due to a leg injury, the general public is still deeply regretful.

Weihai Becomes a Unit

Tianjin Unit Canceled

Jinan, 28th - The North China Annual Meeting will be held at 7:00 PM tonight at the North China Preparatory Committee. The decision was made to cancel the Tianjin unit and establish Weihai as a unit. It is yet to be determined whether Xinjiang and Ningxia will join.

Finals Overview

Jinan, 28th - The situation of the important competitions is as follows:

800-Meter Final: Wang Minshen of Harbin, who had previously clocked 2 minutes and 3 seconds in the 800 meters, was the focus of the crowd's attention. As a result, Wang indeed broke the national record with a time of 2 minutes and 6.8 seconds to win first place. Zhang Xiang of Liaoning emerged as a dark horse and also broke the record with a time of 2 minutes and 7 seconds, trailing by 8 meters. Jiang Yunlong of Liaoning finished third, tying the national record with a time of 2 minutes and 8.4 seconds. Fan Baoen of Beiping finished fourth.

1500-Meter Final: It was initially believed that Jiang Yunlong of Liaoning, who held the national record, would maintain his championship. However, he nearly failed to qualify, falling behind by more than ten places at first. Fortunately, he worked hard and finished fourth. The first place went to the new general Zhang Baoxiang of Liaoning, who broke the national record with a time of 4 minutes and 21 seconds, beating the second place by ten meters. His posture was good, his elasticity was abundant, and with hard practice, he could still improve. Liu Guxue of Liaoning finished second with a time of 4 minutes and 22 seconds, also breaking the national record. Ma Degang competed fiercely with the second place. The four athletes were all from Liaoning.

Senior Discus: It was expected that Zhang Lingjia of Liaoning would break the national record. As a result, he unexpectedly finished second with a time of 35.49 meters. The first place went to Zhou Lianzeng of Liaoning, who achieved a score of 36.50 meters. Yang Xuexian of Shandong finished third with a score of 34.48 meters. Zhao Wenzao of Beiping also scored 33.42 meters for fourth place. Thirty-five people participated.

Women's 50 Meters: Xiao Shuling of Harbin clocked 7.3 seconds in the preliminaries, and Li Bojin of Tianjin clocked 7.3 seconds, both breaking the national record. Wang Yuan of Harbin was also selected for the finals. Both Xiao and Wang failed to win, while Wu Meixian won first place with a time of 7.4 seconds, tying the national record. Li Bojin finished second.

Women's Long Jump: Wu Meixian, the national champion, failed to qualify. The first, second, and third places all broke the national record. A total of 31 people participated. (1) Bian Junian (Tianjin), 4.46 meters; (2) Li Bojin (Tianjin), 4.24 meters; (3) Tong Zhiying (Shandong), 4.11 meters; (4) Yuan Chengxian (Qingdao), 4.07 meters.

Women's 80-Meter Hurdles: In the women's 80-meter hurdles final, the first place went to Zhang Suhui of Shandong, the second place went to Wu Zongwu of Beiping, the third place went to Sun Guiyun of Harbin, and the fourth place went to Sun Yuanshao of Liaoning. The time was 15.2/10 seconds. Sun Guiyun has a reputation as a national female runner, but this time she was defeated by Zhang Suhui of Shandong, which is regrettable. Zhang Suhui's first appearance was a great surprise, which is admirable.

Han Fuju Hosts All Athletes (Photo by Zilin)

International Olympic Games

Chinese Supplementary Representatives

Li Shao Shang's Special Achievement

The supplementary selection of Chinese representatives for the International Olympic Games was held at the Chinese Track and Field Field at 4:00 PM yesterday. The committee members arrived at the field to test the discus and pole vault events. Because the results of the testers were too poor (2.8 meters for pole vault and 2.8 meters for discus), no representatives were selected. Li Shao Shang's special achievement of 2 minutes 14 and 2/5 seconds in the 800 meters was selected as the official representative, adding Chen Xingpei to the list of original runners in the 10,000 meters.

(1) 800 meters: Li Shao Shang; (2) 1500 meters: Zhu Shaohua, Dong Jiaxie; (3) 10,000 meters: Chen Xingpei; (4) Shot Put: Wang Jihuai; (5) High Jump: Gu Yu, Chen Tianhe; (6) Long Jump: Chen Gongyu; (7) Triple Jump: Fan Jiaju, Li Lin; (8) 400-Meter Hurdles: Wu Zuxian

Furthermore, the Sports Association's contribution states that Xie Quanhe, originally selected for pole vaulting, was a mistake for Jiang Shanjing.

Liangjiang Achieves Double Victory in Dalian

Defeats Meisong and Shuming

Dalian, 28th (Guowen News Agency) - On the 27th, the Liangjiang Women's Basketball Team defeated the Meisong Girls' School by 33 to 17. Today, they defeated the Shuming Girls' School by 19 to 12. They will return to Shanghai on the Fengtian Maru on the 1st.

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education issued a notice yesterday stating that the Ministry of Education has repeatedly ordered all levels of private schools in the city to complete the registration procedures by the end of this year's summer vacation, i.e., one day before the start of the first semester of the 20th year. If they still fail to comply by the deadline, strict enforcement will be carried out. The Bureau has repeatedly issued deadlines for the schools to comply. Now that the deadline is approaching, all levels of schools that have not yet applied for registration should immediately follow the procedures prescribed in the Private School Regulations and submit their applications within the deadline. They should not wait and see, so as not to cause trouble for themselves. Please note that this is the final notice. If they fail to comply again, the Bureau will strictly enforce the regulations in order to comply with the Ministry's order and attach importance to education.

Expected to be Implemented on July 1st

Ministry of Communications Streamlines Telecommunications

Shanghai-Fuzhou Lines Being Repaired Quickly

Methods for Communication between Fujian and Taiwan Agreed Upon

More Copper Wires Added to Beijing-Shanghai Telephone Line

The Ministry of Communications has recently been actively streamlining telecommunications matters. According to a person from the Ministry of Communications who came to Shanghai from Beijing yesterday, the Ministry's recent improvements to telecommunications can be divided into four categories: wired telecommunications, wireless telecommunications, underwater telecommunications, and telephone. The plans are described as follows:

Repair Trunk Lines: Regarding wired telecommunications, the Shanghai-Fuzhou telecommunication line has been ordered to be repaired in three sections. The remaining trunk lines between Fuzhou and Guangzhou and between Hankou and Chongqing will be constructed in the shortest possible time. New listening devices will be used, and operators from major bureaus across the country will be ordered to practice listening. A telegram skills competition is also being planned, starting with major bureaus and eventually expanding into a large-scale competition to improve the skills of telegram personnel.

Xiamen-Philippines Communication: Regarding wireless telecommunications, after the receiving and dispatching offices of the underwater wire companies in Fuzhou and Xiamen were taken back, all underwater wire telegrams were changed to be relayed via wired and wireless telecommunications. However, the Shanghai-Fuzhou wired telecommunication line is occasionally out of repair, and the machines at the Fuzhou and Xiamen stations are also small, fearing that they may not be able to cope. Personnel have been sent to install one 100-watt and one 75-watt short-wave machine in Fuzhou. The Xiamen and Taiwan sides have also newly installed 500-watt generators. The Shanghai radio station will greatly renovate its original machine. Furthermore, since communication between Xiamen and the Philippines has been relayed by Hong Kong and Shanghai, there has been a slight delay in time. Recently, an agreement has been made with the Philippines that direct communication is now possible.

Fujian-Taiwan Underwater Line: As for underwater lines, the telegrams between Fujian and Taiwan have been entrusted to the Great East Company by Japan. Now that the Great East contract has expired, the right to relay this information should be taken back by China. An order has been issued by the Ministry to stop the process and to request the representative of Japan to negotiate with the Telegraph Bureau to take over the relay. In order to take care of the communication between Fujian and Taiwan, temporary communication methods have been established.

Beijing-Shanghai Telephone: As for long-distance telephone lines, the Beijing-Shanghai line is the most congested. The original long-distance telephone line between Beijing and Shanghai had three pairs of copper wires. Now, in order to facilitate calls and avoid congestion, materials such as sounding lines have been purchased, and it has been decided to add another pair. Commissioners have been assigned to start construction as soon as possible, and the project will be completed in the shortest possible time.

The Customs has issued announcements on the 15th and 18th of this month. The regulations are now stipulated as follows: For ships heading to foreign ports that have been assigned a customs clearance number, if the export declaration for the local goods loaded on the ship is submitted to the Customs before 4:00 PM on the 30th of this month, the goods will still be subject to export tax and surtax at the current tariff rate. Notice from Jianghai Customs

The General Affairs Department of Jianghai Customs issued a notice yesterday regarding the tax exemption for local silk. The notice stated that a special tax of 30 yuan in national currency per dan was levied on the shipment of yellow and white silk from Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces to foreign countries. The Customs had issued an announcement on the 18th of this month. Now, the Customs Service of the Ministry of Finance has ordered that this special tax will only be levied on factory silk shipped abroad, and all other types of non-factory silk will be exempted. Please be informed accordingly and notify all merchants.

Letter from the Machine Industry Association to the Consolidated Tax Bureau

The Shanghai Machine-Made National Goods Factory Association recently sent a letter to the Consolidated Tax Bureau expressing its opinion that the customs declaration rules established by the Tax Bureau for goods exported overseas, which require the submission of a copy of the bill of lading or pier donation receipt when refunding taxes, are practically difficult to implement. The letter states: "We respectfully report that our members have informed the association that, according to Article 7, Section 4 of the customs declaration rules established by your bureau (details omitted) for the method of refunding the consolidated tax on cotton yarn for various cotton textile products manufactured by factories and exported overseas, 'In addition to filling out the tax refund application form and attaching the original tax payment certificate, it must be submitted to the resident customs office at the original place of shipment for inspection, endorsement, and stamping. The manufacturer shall then present it to the Consolidated Tax Bureau or district office for processing the tax refund according to regulations.' There is no mention of submitting a copy of the bill of lading from the shipping company. However, the application form for the tax refund on exported cotton yarn directly woven into finished products includes the words 'Attached is a copy of the bill of lading.' Moreover, the copy of the bill of lading for goods exported overseas and taxed according to regulations has a green wooden stamp that says, 'This bill of lading is only for the Consolidated Tax Bureau's retention and shall not be used as collateral by anyone, Chinese or foreign.' The receipt for the customs pier donation also has the stamp 'Approved for export tax refund by the Resident Customs Office of the Consolidated Tax Bureau of the Ministry of Finance at the Jianghai Customs.' Following the above procedures would cause difficulties. Submitting a copy of the bill of lading or pier donation receipt is practically impossible for the following reasons: (1) A copy of the bill of lading is traditionally kept as proof for retrieving goods in case the original is lost. (2) Merchants from distant regions often send the original bill of lading with the goods and mail the copy separately to prevent delays in sales if the original is lost. (3) If merchants from other provinces purchase goods such as towels and load them along with dozens of other types of miscellaneous goods into several boxes, the shipping company will issue only one set of original and duplicate bills of lading, which will also cause related difficulties. (4) Both the original and duplicate bills of lading for goods used for foreign exchange settlements must be submitted to the bank to comply with the settlement procedures. (5) The stamp on the copy of the bill of lading stating that 'This bill of lading shall not be used as collateral by anyone, Chinese or foreign' effectively deprives the merchant of their right to use it as collateral. (6) The receipt for the customs pier donation or dredging donation serves as proof for the company or business to reconcile accounts. The above difficulties sufficiently prove that the copy of the bill of lading or pier donation receipt should be kept by the merchant. According to our association's humble opinion, when cotton yarn or cotton yarn directly woven into finished products that have already paid the consolidated tax are exported overseas, the customs should only need to inspect the tax payment certificate and attached documents. The customs should then issue a certificate for the refund of the consolidated tax on the exported cotton yarn. The manufacturer can then use this certificate to claim the tax refund from the Consolidated Tax Bureau or district office. This is both convenient and free from corruption. We hope that our humble suggestion will be adopted. We respectfully submit this letter in the hope that it will be reviewed and approved."

The Ministry of Finance replied yesterday to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce's telegram, stating: "We have reviewed the Dongdai telegram from the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce regarding the request to exempt the business tax on exported tea chests. Continued Intrusion of Japanese Vessels in Shanghai Waters

The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Agriculture and Mining has submitted reports to the Provincial Government and the Ministry of Industry for review.

In order to protect coastal fisheries in Jiangsu Province, the Provincial Government previously convened a Fisheries Protection Conference. Regarding the prevention of intrusion by foreign vessels, two measures were resolved, including the provision that the Department of Agriculture and Mining would regularly submit reports on the situation of Japanese fishing vessels' intrusion, based on investigations. The Provincial Government instructed the Department of Agriculture to comply accordingly. According to the Department's investigation, since May 1st of this year, there have been twelve Japanese fishing vessels, including the Man Qian Maru and Zhou Fang Maru, entering and leaving Shanghai ports and dumping their catch. In addition, there are more than twenty vessels, including the Da Cheng Maru, which had previously been engaged in intrusion and are temporarily waiting and watching, fearing that Chinese customs will prohibit their import on schedule. If this situation is not resolved in the shortest possible time, the continuous arrival of Japanese vessels in Shanghai is expected. It is reported that the Department has submitted reports to the Provincial Government and the Ministry of Industry for review.

The Qu Case to be Heard in Military Court

Anhui Fellow Provincials Decide on Assistance Measures

The Ta Mei Evening News reports that U.S. military personnel involved in the stabbing injury case of Qu Shixiang, owner of a clothing store at the intersection of Avenue Edward VII and Gordon Road, and others, will be tried in a public military court, according to Colonel Hawke, commander of the U.S. Marine Corps, this morning (the 28th). Journalists and people from all countries will be allowed to attend the hearing. However, Colonel Hawke did not specify the date of the trial or the charges.

The case of the U.S. sailors stabbing Qu Shixiang, the owner of the Qu Shunji clothing store, his son, and his associate Ma Ruixiang on Avenue Edward VII and Gordon Road has aroused great indignation in all circles. The Anhui Shanghai Fellow-Provincials Association held an executive meeting yesterday, chaired by Liu Zuwang, and resolved the following assistance measures: (1) Send a letter to the Diplomatic Commissioner's Office in Shanghai lodging a serious protest. (2) Send a letter to the Shanghai Bar Association requesting legal assistance according to the law. (3) Send a letter to the police requesting attention to the evidence of the assault. (4) Send a letter to Baolong Hospital requesting that the injured be given medical attention. At the same time, Zhu Runbin and Peng Tiancheng were dispatched to the hospital together with reporters Ding Zigu, Wang Haiqing, and Wang Zhaoyong to investigate the injuries of Qu Shixiang and Ma Ruixiang. According to their investigation report, Qu Shixiang, a native of Tongcheng, 41 years old, was stabbed by an American soldier with a knife, which entered directly from the left temple to the ear, and his left arm was also injured. His injuries are extremely serious. He is still able to speak, but not much. Ma Ruixiang, a native of Hefei, was stabbed in the neck and the wound reached the oral cavity. He is unable to speak, and his injuries are also very critical. Dr. Li Zongwei of the hospital stated that although Qu is able to speak, the wound is in a vital area, and his life may be in danger. Ma's injury is not as vital, but the injury is also severe, and his life may also be difficult to save. The association investigated and requested to take photographs, but other doctors stated that the injured person's wound is still being stitched and dressed, and cannot be exposed to the wind, as it may endanger their lives. Permission was given to delay the photographs for a while. The circumstances of Qu and Ma's stabbing by the American soldiers are generally the same as reported in the newspapers. In addition to emergency assistance, the association will also report to the executive and supervisory committees for active negotiation and request the unified support of all sectors to protect the lives and safety of fellow provincials in the concession. It is also reported that Qu Haigou, whose name is not known, is currently at home.

Gu Case

The Support Association Held its First Meeting Yesterday

Appointing Organizational Personnel

Sending Representatives to Petition in Beijing

The Shanghai All-Circles Support Association for the Gu Jingen Tragedy held its first executive committee meeting at the Postal Workers Union in Xingjia Muqiao yesterday afternoon. More than 20 representatives from party branches and labor unions attended. The meeting commenced at about 3 o'clock, with Chen Weiyi presiding. The meeting resolved to appoint staff and pass a declaration, among other important matters. The details of the meeting are recorded below:

Matters Resolved: The Shanghai All-Circles Support Association for the Gu Jingen Tragedy held its first executive committee meeting at 3:00 PM yesterday afternoon, presided over by Chen Weiyi. Discussion Items: (1) Regarding the establishment of the organization and appointment of personnel, it was resolved to appoint Zhao Shusheng, Wang Wenhua, Chen Weiyi, Zhu Pingan, and Li Yongxiang as standing committee members, and Zhao Shusheng as the director of the secretariat, Wang Wenhua as the director of the general affairs department, Chen Weiyi as the director of the publicity department, and Wang Xiaolai as the director of the public relations department. (2) Regarding the appointment of deputy directors for each department, it was resolved to appoint Shen Dinglu and Mu Qin as deputy directors of the secretariat, Zhu Pingan and Li Yongxiang as deputy directors of the public relations department, Tang Junsheng and Fang Xuexiang as deputy directors of the general affairs department, and the Bar Association and the Chinese Taxpayers Association as deputy directors of the publicity department. (3) Regarding the constitution of the association, it was resolved that the association's constitution would use the name "Shanghai All-Circles Support Association for the Gu Jingen Tragedy" and be handled by the general affairs department. (4) The association's declaration was passed (resolved) with revisions. (5) Zhao Shusheng proposed hiring Lawyer Wu Mai as the association's legal advisor. The resolution was passed. (6) Regarding the discussion of the advance payment and attached receipts from Taichang Construction Company, the discussion was postponed. (7) Regarding the request to send representatives to Beijing to petition the National Government to order the court to bring the murderers to Chinese courts for trial, it was resolved to pass it. Wang Xiaolai, Wang Wenhua, and Zhu Pingan were appointed as representatives, and Comrade Wu Mai was invited to be an advisor. Zhao Shusheng was appointed as an alternate representative. (8) Regarding the request to send representatives to negotiate with the U.S. Minister and Consul in Shanghai, the resolution was the same as item (7). (9) Regarding the assignment of personnel to contact Lawyer You Niqian, the resolution was passed and assigned to the public relations department. (10) Regarding the location of the association, it was resolved to use the Postal Workers Union in Xingjia Muqiao, Qiujiang Road, Shanghai. (11) Regarding the date of the executive committee's regular meeting, it was decided to be at 2:00 PM every Thursday. It was resolved that if the goal is not achieved, the association will, together with the national public, automatically sever relations with the United States.

Declaration Published: The Shanghai All-Circles Support Association for the Gu Jingen Tragedy Declaration was revised and passed at yesterday's first meeting. The original text is as follows: Gu Jingen, a carpenter from Taichang Construction Company, was shot and killed by U.S. sailors in his workshop bedroom on the evening of the 22nd of last month. Nine other carpenters were sleeping in the same room with Gu that day, and they were all spared from the disaster. The tragic news spread, and the world was filled with indignation. Sailors, whose duty it is to protect the peace, recklessly shot and killed innocent, unarmed civilians. It seems that they not only treat the lives of our people as if they were grass, but they are also public enemies of our nation (details omitted). Recalling the shadows of past tragedies, witnessing the frequency of today's disasters, and speculating on the hidden worries of the future, this association cannot help but be filled with trembling fear. We use the spirit of universal love and equality to shout out our national hatred: (1) Severely punish the murderers. The criminals should be submitted to our courts for severe punishment in accordance with the order of our government on January 1, 1930, and the recovery of judicial sovereignty. (2) Punish the officers. The U.S. sailors recklessly caused a major disaster of murder. The senior officers in charge are responsible for negligence, and at the very least, they should be dismissed and punished. (3) Compensation and condolence. The U.S. government is responsible for compensating the losses of the deceased with 100,000 yuan and consoling the family of the deceased with 20,000 yuan. (4) Formal apology. The U.S. government should formally apologize to the National Government for the occurrence of this tragedy and clearly state the measures to prevent and guarantee similar tragedies in the future. These four points are all passive and the minimum of follow-up measures, and they are what this association vows to strive for with all our might. Even more regrettable is that, following the Gu case, the U.S. sailors' barbarous and reckless provocations continue to occur one after another, such as two sailors fighting each other, angering a small worker and pushing him into the water to drown, and two sailors randomly stabbing Qu Shixiang and his store associate Mr. Ma with knives. If a fundamental prevention plan is not devised, the occurrence of tragic events will only increase. Tracing back to the root cause, it is the evil concessions and consular jurisdiction that are the root causes. These two are the most harmful poisons in the unequal treaties and the best tools for imperialist aggression against our country. Without recovering the concessions and abolishing consular jurisdiction, it is not enough to abolish the unequal treaties, and it is even less enough to eradicate the poison of imperialism. The National Assembly first took the abolition of unequal treaties as its banner and declared its determination to the world. This is a plan to learn from the past, prevent future occurrences, and achieve long-term stability. This association deeply hopes that the entire nation will be of one mind and support the resolutions of the National Assembly, urging the party branch to assist the government to implement them effectively. We also hope that our civilized allies will be enlightened by the happiness of freedom and equality and automatically wash away the sins of imperialism so that the bloody tragedy of mutual slaughter will never be seen again in Chinese territory. So that our Republic of China can establish equal friendship with all countries in the world, and shine brightly and illuminate the universe. All of us Chinese people must vow to strive with all our might to achieve the goals of this association, and we will not hesitate to make any sacrifice. This association respectfully represents all sectors of Shanghai in declaring our peaceful goodwill, and we hope that all compatriots in the country and friends from all over the world will take note. This declaration is hereby made by the Shanghai All-Circles Support Association for the Gu Jingen Tragedy on May 28, 1931.
